<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заморозка.html>заморозок</a> (30628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заморозить.html>заморо́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamorózitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заморозка.html>за́морозок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zámorozok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заморозка.html>за́морозка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заморозка.html>за́морозки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заморозок.html>за́морозков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">meteorology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> overnight freeze, cold snap <i>(usually in late spring or early autumn, when days are warm)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***замотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замотать.html>замота́ть</a> (9054)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мотать.html>мота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">motátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замотать.html>замота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зама́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to roll up, to fold up</li>
<li>to twist <i>(round)</i>, to wind <i>(round)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out, to tire out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to withhold, to refuse to give, to appropriate, to help oneself, to hook</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tie up, to bind up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замотать.html>замота́ли</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá sovsém déla <b>zamotáli</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I am completely tied up with (bound up in; snowed under with) my affairs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shake, to begin to shake
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замотать.html>замота́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голово́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamotátʹ</b> golovój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to (begin to) shake one's head</span></div></dd>

***замочить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a> (12446)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочить.html>мочи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">močítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamočítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочить.html>мочи́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зама́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamočítʹ</b> nogi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wet one's feet; get one's feet wet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to soak, to steep
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:белье.html>бельё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamočítʹ</b> belʹjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to soak the washing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></b> лён (<a href = vnd.unilang:конопля.html>коноплю́</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamočítʹ</b> ljón (konopljú)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ret flax (hemp)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замочить.html>замочи́ть</a></b> со́лод</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamočítʹ</b> sólod</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to liquor malt</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do <i>(for)</i>, to do in, to bump off, to polish off, to take for a ride</li></ol>

<ul><li>From <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>behind</i>) + <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">муж</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">muž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>husband</i>), lit. "behind the husband".</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замуж.html>за́муж</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zámuž</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>married (<i>of women only</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выходить.html>выходи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замуж.html>за́муж</a></b> (impf.) / <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йти</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замуж.html>за́муж</a></b> (pf) (<a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vyxodítʹ <b>zámuž</b> (impf.) / výjti <b>zámuž</b> (pf) (za)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to marry (a man) + accusative case)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́шла</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замуж.html>за́муж</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Za kovó oná výšla <b>zámuž</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Who did she <b>marry</b>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замужем.html>за́мужем</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zámužem</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>of women</i> - married (state), adverb)</li>

***замуровать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замуровать.html>замурова́ть</a> (21972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мурова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">murovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замуровать.html>замурова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamurovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замуро́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to seal (a hole or opening with masonry)</li>
<li>to immure <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to cloister someone behind walls, or to hide something inside of a wall</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замуровать.html>замурова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клад.html>клад</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>стене́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamurovátʹ</b> klad v stené</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>immure/hide</b> the treasure in a wall</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prevent (someone) from freely communicating or moving</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замуро́вываться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamuróvyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замурова́ться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamurovátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замуро́вывание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamuróvyvanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">замуро́вка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zamuróvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замутить.html>замути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stir up, to make turbid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мутить.html>мути́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>во́ду</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:водоем.html>водоёме</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mutítʹ vódu (v vodojóme)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">muddy the waters</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:замутить.html>замутит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on vody ne zamutit</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> he is as meek as a lamb; he wouldn't hurt a fly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The expression <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:замутить.html>замути́т</a></span>, about a quiet man, is always accented as such.
</p>

***замучить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замучить.html>заму́чить</a> (8435)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">múčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замучить.html>заму́чить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamúčitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заму́чивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to torture, to torment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замучить.html>заму́чить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamúčitʹ</b> dó smerti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to torture to death</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tire out, to wear out, to bore, to weary</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучить.html>му́чить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">múčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучиться.html>му́читься</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">múčitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучитель.html>мучи́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mučítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучительно.html>мучи́тельно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mučítelʹno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучительный.html>мучи́тельный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mučítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:му.html>му́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чить</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — замучивать.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>за-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-муч-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замучиться.html>заму́читься</a> (30986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замучить.html>заму́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamúčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замучиться.html>заму́читься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamúčitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мучиться.html>му́читься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to agonize, to be exhausted, to distress oneself, to be fed up, to be worn out</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">замше́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamšétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become mossy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замшелый.html>замше́лый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamšélyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mossy, moss-grown</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> moss-grown, old-fashioned; set in one's ways</li></ol>

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкаться.html>замыка́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamykátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a> (14675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мыка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamykátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуть.html>замкну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lock</li>
<li>to close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цепь.html>цепь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamykátʹ</b> cepʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to close the circuit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go last
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:колонна.html>коло́нну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamykátʹ</b> šéstvije, kolónnu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bring up the rear; close the file</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкаться.html>замыка́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zamykátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замкнуться.html>замкну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lock, to be locked</li>
<li>to be closed, to close <i>(up)</i></li>
<li>to become/be sullen/withdrawn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкаться.html>замыка́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкаться.html>замыка́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свою́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорлупа.html>скорлупу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zamykatʹsja</b> v sebé; <b>zamykatʹsja</b> v svojú skorlupú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to withdraw/retreat into oneself; go into one's shell</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замыкать.html>замыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zamykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
